                          <section class="col-12  ">
            <div id="content" class="block system_main_block block-system">
  
    
      

<div id="system-main" class="block system">   <article class="node--event">
    <div class="row">
      <div class="col-12 col-lg-8 ">
        <div class="row mb-3">
                      <div class="col-12 order-2">
                              
<h1 data-component-id="um_base:title" class="title title--xl">
  
    JURIX 2023

  </h1>
                          </div>
                                      <div class="col-12 order-3 mt-2">
                  <i class="fa-regular fa-calendar-day me-1"></i> 
      <time datetime="2023-12-17T23:00:00Z">18 December 2023 00:00</time>
 - <time datetime="2023-12-19T23:00:00Z">20 December 2023 00:00</time>

  
              </div>
                              </div>

                  <div class="row mb-4 row-gap-4">
                                          <div class="col-12">
                  <p><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span>36th International Conference on Legal Knowledge and Information Systems.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
                </div>
                                            <div class="col-12">
                  <div class="paragraphs paragraphs--top">
      

  
  
  <section class="paragraph paragraph--type--text mb-6">
                    
      <p><span lang="EN-GB"><span><a href="https://jurix23.maastrichtlawtech.eu/">Click here to go to the Jurix website (extra info &amp; registration)</a></span></span></p>

<p><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span>This year, JURIX conference on Legal Knowledge and Information Systems will be hosted in Maastricht, the Netherlands (Faculty of Law, Maastricht) and&nbsp;will take place from 18 to 20 December, 2023.</span></span></span></span><br>
<span><span><span><span>The Foundation for Legal Knowledge Based Systems (JURIX) is an </span></span></span></span><span><span><span><span>organisation</span></span></span></span><span><span><span><span> of researchers in the field of Law and Computer Science in the Netherlands and Flanders. Since 1988, JURIX has held annual international conferences on Legal Knowledge and Information Systems.&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span>The proceedings of the conferences will be published in the Frontiers of Artificial Intelligence and Applications series of IOS Press. JURIX follows the Golden Standard and provides one of the best dissemination platforms in AI &amp; law.&nbsp;<br>
<br>
<strong>You can click on the oker and green buttons on the right side to find more detailed information about the event and to register.</strong></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><strong>About the Event Organizer</strong></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span>Maastricht University (UM) is the most international university in the Netherlands and, with nearly 22,000 students and 4,400 employees, is still growing. The university distinguishes itself with its innovative education model, international character and multidisciplinary approach to research and education. Today, it is considered one of the best young universities in the world. </span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span>The local organizer of JURIX 2023 â€“ </span></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><a href="https://www.maastrichtuniversity.nl/about-um/faculties/law/research/law-and-tech-lab">Maastricht Law and Tech Lab </a></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><span>â€“ fosters a community of legal researchers and computer scientists who work collaboratively to integrate law and computer science methods.â€‹&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><strong>Registration</strong></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><span><strong>Please click on the green button on the right side in order to register.</strong> Note that early registration rates apply until 30 November 2023. The proceedings will be published after the conference (see 'Proceedings').&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
  

                </section>

      

  
  
  <section class="paragraph paragraph--type--image mb-6">
                    <div class="paragraph-content">
    <div class="row">
      <div class="col-12">
